Accessibility digest

Synopsis
PageHeritage Operations Group
URLhttps://www.heritageofcare.com/
Requesterpool@jpdev.pro

Score1096
Tested byTestaro, procedure ts24
Scored byTestilo, procedure tsp24
Digested byTestilo, procedure tdp24

Introduction

This is a digest of results from a battery of accessibility Tests.

The battery includes 1353 automated accessibility tests drawn from ten different packages: Alfa, Axe, Continuum, Equal Access, HTML CodeSniffer, Nu Html Checker, QualWeb, Tenon, Testaro, and WAVE.

These tests were run on the web page named above and gave the page a score of 1096, where 0 would be perfect.

Issue summary

Special issues

log: Score 335. This is based on the amount of browser error logging and miscellaneous logging during the tests.

Classified issues

Issue textContrastAA

WCAG: 1.4.3

Score: 90

Issue reports in this category:

  • Package alfa, test r69, score 52 (Text outside widget has subminimum contrast)
  • Package axe, test color-contrast, score 47 (Element has insufficient color contrast)
  • Package htmlcs, test e:AAA.1_4_6.G18.Fail, score 4 (Contrast between the text and its background is less than 4.5:1)
  • Package wave, test c:contrast, score 39 (Very low contrast)

Issue linkIndication

WCAG: 1.3.3

Score: 88

Issue reports in this category:

  • Package testaro, test linkUl, score 86 (Non-underlined adjacent links)

Issue duplicateID

WCAG: 4.1.1

Score: 61

Issue reports in this category:

  • Package alfa, test r3, score 32 (Element id attribute value is not unique)
  • Package axe, test duplicate-id-aria, score 4 (id attribute used in ARIA or in a label has a value that is not unique)
  • Package axe, test duplicate-id, score 3 (id attribute value is not unique)
  • Package continuum, test 94, score 32 (Element contains an id attribute set to a value that is not unique in the DOM)
  • Package htmlcs, test e:AAA.4_1_1.F77, score 16 (Duplicate id attribute value)
  • Package ibm, test RPT_Elem_UniqueId, score 12 (Element id attribute value is not unique within the document)

Score: 40

Issue reports in this category:

  • Package qualWeb, test QW-ACT-R62, score 34 (Element in the sequential focus order has no visible focus)
